         from flask import Flask, request, redirect, url_for, render_template, session, abort
         from datetime import datetime
         import os
         import threading
         import difflib
         
         # Flask app initialization
         app = Flask(__name__)
         app.secret_key = 'a_very_secret_key_for_session_management_change_me'  # For session management
         
         DATA_DIR = 'data'
         LOCK = threading.Lock()  # Global lock for file write operations
         
         # Helper function to parse pipe-delimited text files into list of dicts
         # fields is a list of field names
         
         def read_pipe_delimited_file(filename, fields):
             records = []
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, filename)
             if not os.path.exists(filepath):
                 return records
             with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for line in f:
                     line=line.strip()
                     if not line:
                         continue
                     parts = line.split('|')
                     if len(parts) < len(fields):
                         # malformed line - skip
                         continue
                     rec = dict(zip(fields, parts))
                     records.append(rec)
             return records
         
         # Helper function to append a record (dict) to pipe-delimited file
         # fields order needed
         
         def append_pipe_delimited_file(filename, fields, record):
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, filename)
             with LOCK:
                 with open(filepath, 'a', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     line = '|'.join(str(record.get(field, '')).replace('\n',' ') for field in fields) + '\n'
                     f.write(line)
         
         # Helper function to overwrite whole file (list of dicts)
         def overwrite_pipe_delimited_file(filename, fields, records):
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, filename)
             with LOCK:
                 with open(filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for record in records:
                         line = '|'.join(str(record.get(field, '')).replace('\n',' ') for field in fields) + '\n'
                         f.write(line)
         
         ############################
         # User Model
         ############################
         # users.txt fields:
         # id|username|role
         USER_FIELDS = ['id','username','role']
         
         def get_all_users():
             return read_pipe_delimited_file('users.txt', USER_FIELDS)
         
         def get_user_by_username(username):
             users = get_all_users()
             for u in users:
                 if u['username'] == username:
                     return u
             return None
         
         ############################
         # Article Model
         ############################
         # articles.txt fields:
         # article_id|title|author|category|status|created_date|last_modified
         ARTICLE_FIELDS = ['article_id','title','author','category','status','created_date','last_modified']
         
         def get_all_articles():
             return read_pipe_delimited_file('articles.txt', ARTICLE_FIELDS)
         
         def get_article_by_id(article_id):
             articles = get_all_articles()
             for a in articles:
                 if a['article_id'] == str(article_id):
                     return a
             return None
         
         # Update article in articles.txt by article_id
         def update_article(article_id, title=None, category=None, status=None, last_modified=None):
             articles = get_all_articles()
             updated = False
             for a in articles:
                 if a['article_id'] == str(article_id):
                     if title is not None:
                         a['title'] = title
                     if category is not None:
                         a['category'] = category
                     if status is not None:
                         a['status'] = status
                     if last_modified is not None:
                         a['last_modified'] = last_modified
                     updated = True
                     break
             if updated:
                 overwrite_pipe_delimited_file('articles.txt', ARTICLE_FIELDS, articles)
             return updated
         
         # Create new article
         # Returns article_id assigned
         # article_id assigned auto-increment max existing + 1
         
         def create_article(title, author, category):
             articles = get_all_articles()
             if articles:
                 max_id = max(int(a['article_id']) for a in articles)
             else:
                 max_id = 0
             new_id = max_id + 1
             now_str = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')
             new_article = {
                 'article_id': str(new_id),
                 'title': title,
                 'author': author,
                 'category': category if category else '',
                 'status': 'draft',
                 'created_date': now_str,
                 'last_modified': now_str
             }
             append_pipe_delimited_file('articles.txt', ARTICLE_FIELDS, new_article)
             return new_id
         
         ############################
         # Article Versions Model
         ############################
         # article_versions.txt fields:
         # version_id|article_id|version_number|content|author|created_date|change_summary
         ARTICLE_VERSION_FIELDS = ['version_id','article_id','version_number','content','author','created_date','change_summary']
         
         def get_all_article_versions():
             return read_pipe_delimited_file('article_versions.txt', ARTICLE_VERSION_FIELDS)
         
         def get_versions_by_article_id(article_id):
             versions = get_all_article_versions()
             result = [v for v in versions if v['article_id'] == str(article_id)]
             # Sort by version_number ascending
             result.sort(key=lambda x: int(x['version_number']))
             return result
         
         # Get latest version for article_id
         # returns None if none found
         
         def get_latest_version(article_id):
             versions = get_versions_by_article_id(article_id)
             if not versions:
                 return None
             return versions[-1]
         
         # Create new version for article
         # version_number auto-incremented
         
         def create_new_version(article_id, content, author, change_summary):
             versions = get_versions_by_article_id(article_id)
             if versions:
                 max_version = max(int(v['version_number']) for v in versions)
             else:
                 max_version = 0
             new_version_num = max_version + 1
             # version_id assigned as max existing + 1 (global)
             all_versions = get_all_article_versions()
             if all_versions:
                 max_version_id = max(int(v['version_id']) for v in all_versions)
             else:
                 max_version_id = 0
             new_version_id = max_version_id + 1
             now_str = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')
             new_version = {
                 'version_id': str(new_version_id),
                 'article_id': str(article_id),
                 'version_number': str(new_version_num),
                 'content': content,
                 'author': author,
                 'created_date': now_str,
                 'change_summary': change_summary if change_summary else ''
             }
             append_pipe_delimited_file('article_versions.txt', ARTICLE_VERSION_FIELDS, new_version)
             return new_version

         ############################
         # analytics.txt fields:
         # analytics_id|article_id|views|unique_visitors|avg_time_on_article|shares|date
         ANALYTICS_FIELDS = ['analytics_id','article_id','views','unique_visitors','avg_time_on_article','shares','date']
         
         def get_all_analytics():
             return read_pipe_delimited_file('analytics.txt', ANALYTICS_FIELDS)
         
         def get_analytics_by_article(article_id):
             analytics = get_all_analytics()
             filtered = [a for a in analytics if a['article_id'] == str(article_id)]
             return filtered
         
         # Aggregate analytics for an article across all dates
         
         def aggregate_analytics(article_id):
             records = get_analytics_by_article(article_id)
             total_views = 0
             unique_visitors_set = set()
             total_time = 0.0
             total_shares = 0
             count = 0
             for rec in records:
                 total_views += int(rec['views']) if rec['views'].isdigit() else 0
                 unique_visitors_set.add(rec['date'])  # Count unique days as proxy for unique visitors
                 try:
                     t = float(rec['avg_time_on_article'])
                 except:
                     t = 0
                 total_time += t
                 total_shares += int(rec['shares']) if rec['shares'].isdigit() else 0
                 count += 1
             avg_time = (total_time/count) if count > 0 else 0
             analytics_summary = {
                 'total_views': total_views,
                 'unique_visitors_count': len(unique_visitors_set),
                 'average_time_on_article': round(avg_time,2),
                 'total_shares': total_shares
             }
             return analytics_summary
         
         ############################
         # Version Control Util Functions
         ############################
         # Generate diff summary between two versions (old_content, new_content)
         def generate_diff_summary(old_content, new_content):
             old_lines = old_content.splitlines()
             new_lines = new_content.splitlines()
             diff = difflib.unified_diff(old_lines, new_lines, lineterm='')
             diff_text = '\n'.join(diff)
             # For brevity, just return diff as a string
             return diff_text
         
         ############################
         # Authentication & Session Helpers
         ############################
         # For demonstration, simulate logged in user from session
         
         def get_logged_in_username():
             # In real app, use flask-login or similar
             if 'username' in session:
                 return session['username']
             return None

         # Routes Implementation
         ############################
         
         @app.route('/')
         def root_redirect():
             return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))
         
         
         @app.route('/dashboard')
         def dashboard():
             username = get_logged_in_username()
             if not username:
                 return redirect(url_for('root_redirect'))
             # Quick stats and recent activity for user
             # Quick stats: number of articles user authored, articles published, articles in approval
             all_articles = get_all_articles()
             user_articles = [a for a in all_articles if a['author'] == username]
             published_count = sum(1 for a in user_articles if a['status'] == 'published')
             in_approval_count = sum(1 for a in user_articles if a['status'] == 'in_approval')
             quick_stats = {
                 'total_articles': len(user_articles),
                 'published_articles': published_count,
                 'in_approval_articles': in_approval_count
             }
             # Recent activity: last 5 edited or created articles
             user_articles_sorted = sorted(user_articles, key=lambda a: a['last_modified'], reverse=True)[:5]
             recent_activity = []
             for a in user_articles_sorted:
                 recent_activity.append({
                     'article_id': a['article_id'],
                     'title': a['title'],
                     'status': a['status'],
                     'last_modified': a['last_modified']
                 })
             # Render dashboard template with these variables
             return render_template('dashboard.html', username=username, quick_stats=quick_stats, recent_activity=recent_activity)
         
         
         @app.route('/article/create', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def create_article():
             username = get_logged_in_username()
             if not username:
                 return redirect(url_for('root_redirect'))
         
             if request.method == 'GET':
                 return render_template('article_create.html')
         
             # POST method
             title = request.form.get('article_title', '').strip()
             content = request.form.get('article_content', '').strip()
             category = request.form.get('category', '').strip()  # Optional category
         
             errors = []
             if not title:
                 errors.append('Title is required.')
             if not content:
                 errors.append('Content is required.')
         
             if errors:
                 return render_template('article_create.html', errors=errors, article_title=title, article_content=content, category=category)
         
             # Create article record
             new_article_id = create_article(title, username, category)
         
             # Create initial version with version 1
             change_summary = 'Initial version'
             create_new_version(new_article_id, content, username, change_summary)
         
             success_msg = 'Article created successfully.'
             return render_template('article_create.html', success=success_msg)
         
         
         @app.route('/article/<int:article_id>/edit', methods=['GET','POST'])
         def edit_article(article_id):
             username = get_logged_in_username()
             if not username:
                 return redirect(url_for('root_redirect'))
         
             article = get_article_by_id(article_id)
             if not article:
                 abort(404, description='Article not found')
             if article['author'] != username:
                 abort(403, description='Permission denied. Can only edit your own articles.')
         
             if request.method == 'GET':
                 # Load latest version content
                 latest_version = get_latest_version(article_id)
                 content = latest_version['content'] if latest_version else ''
                 title = article['title']
                 return render_template('article_edit.html', article_id=article_id, title=title, content=content)
         
             # POST method
             new_title = request.form.get('article_title', '').strip()
             content = request.form.get('article_content', '').strip()
             category = request.form.get('category', '').strip()  # optional
             change_summary = request.form.get('change_summary', '').strip()  # descriptive summary of edits
         
             errors = []
             if not new_title:
                 errors.append('Title is required.')
             if not content:
                 errors.append('Content is required.')
             if not change_summary:
                 errors.append('Change summary is required.')
         
             if errors:
                 return render_template('article_edit.html', article_id=article_id, title=new_title, content=content, errors=errors)
         
             # Save new version
             new_version = create_new_version(article_id, content, username, change_summary)
         
             # Update article title, category and last_modified date
             now_str = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')
             update_article(article_id, title=new_title, category=category if category else None, last_modified=now_str)
         
             success_msg = 'Article updated and new version saved successfully.'
             return render_template('article_edit.html', article_id=article_id, title=new_title, content=content, success=success_msg)
         
         
         @app.route('/article/<int:article_id>/versions', methods=['GET'])
         def article_version_history(article_id):
             username = get_logged_in_username()
             if not username:
                 return redirect(url_for('root_redirect'))
         
             article = get_article_by_id(article_id)
             if not article:
                 abort(404, description='Article not found')
         
             versions = get_versions_by_article_id(article_id)
             if not versions:
                 versions = []
             # current_version is the highest version number
             current_version = max((int(v['version_number']) for v in versions), default=0)
         
             # Prepare a comparison dict with diffs for each pair of consecutive versions
             comparison = {}
             for i in range(1, len(versions)):
                 v_old = versions[i-1]
                 v_new = versions[i]
                 diff_summary = generate_diff_summary(v_old['content'], v_new['content'])
                 comparison_key = f"{v_old['version_number']}_to_{v_new['version_number']}"
                 comparison[comparison_key] = diff_summary
         
             return render_template('article_versions.html',
                                    article_id=article_id,
                                    versions=versions,
                                    comparison=comparison,
                                    current_version=current_version)
         
         
         @app.route('/articles/mine', methods=['GET'])
         def my_articles():
             username = get_logged_in_username()
             if not username:
                 return redirect(url_for('root_redirect'))
         
             filter_status = request.args.get('status', '').strip().lower()
             all_articles = get_all_articles()
             user_articles = [a for a in all_articles if a['author'] == username]
         
             if filter_status:
                 user_articles = [a for a in user_articles if a['status'].lower() == filter_status]
         
             # Render with articles and filter_status
             return render_template('articles_mine.html', articles=user_articles, filter_status=filter_status)
         
         
         @app.route('/articles/published', methods=['GET'])
         def published_articles():
             filter_category = request.args.get('filter_category', '').strip().lower()
             sort_option = request.args.get('sort_option', '').strip().lower()
         
             all_articles = get_all_articles()
             published_articles = [a for a in all_articles if a['status'] == 'published']
         
             if filter_category:
                 published_articles = [a for a in published_articles if a['category'].lower() == filter_category]
         
             if sort_option == 'date_desc':
                 published_articles.sort(key=lambda a: a['created_date'], reverse=True)
             elif sort_option == 'date_asc':
                 published_articles.sort(key=lambda a: a['created_date'])
             elif sort_option == 'title_asc':
                 published_articles.sort(key=lambda a: a['title'].lower())
             elif sort_option == 'title_desc':
                 published_articles.sort(key=lambda a: a['title'].lower(), reverse=True)
         
             return render_template('articles_published.html',
                                    articles=published_articles,
                                    filter_category=filter_category,
                                    sort_option=sort_option)
         
         
         @app.route('/calendar', methods=['GET','POST'])
         def content_calendar():
             username = get_logged_in_username()
             if not username:
                 return redirect(url_for('root_redirect'))
         
             # For this app, we don't have detail of calendar event schema
             # We keep a simple calendar_data list stored in memory or loaded/saved from a file events.txt (not specified)
             # Here we simulate with empty or fixed data
         
             calendar_data = []
             calendar_view = 'month'  # For example
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 # For demonstration, read new event data from form (e.g., event_name, date)
                 event_name = request.form.get('event_name', '').strip()
                 event_date = request.form.get('event_date', '').strip()
                 # Normally, would add event to persistent storage, but data file schema not defined, so this is stub
                 # Return calendar with confirmation
                 success_msg = 'Event added successfully (stub, not persisted)'
                 return render_template('calendar.html', calendar_view=calendar_view, calendar_data=calendar_data, success=success_msg)
         
             return render_template('calendar.html', calendar_view=calendar_view, calendar_data=calendar_data)
         
         
         @app.route('/article/<int:article_id>/analytics', methods=['GET'])

         # Additional routes for approval and comments for completeness
         
         @app.route('/article/<int:article_id>/version/<int:version_id>/approve', methods=['POST'])
         def approve_version(article_id, version_id):
             username = get_logged_in_username()
             if not username:
                 return redirect(url_for('root_redirect'))
         
             status = request.form.get('status','').strip().lower()  # expected: approved, rejected, revision_requested
             comment = request.form.get('comment','').strip()
             if status not in ['approved','rejected','revision_requested']:
                 return {'error': 'Invalid status value'}, 400
         
             approval = create_approval(article_id, version_id, username, status, comment)
         
             # Service logic to move article through workflow stages would go here (not implemented in full)
         
             return {'message': 'Approval recorded', 'approval': approval}, 200
         
         
         @app.route('/article/<int:article_id>/version/<int:version_id>/comments', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def comments(article_id, version_id):
             username = get_logged_in_username()
             if not username:
                 return redirect(url_for('root_redirect'))
         
             if request.method == 'GET':
                 comments_list = get_comments_by_article_and_version(article_id, version_id)
                 return render_template('comments.html', article_id=article_id, version_id=version_id, comments=comments_list)
         
             # POST method to add comment
             comment_text = request.form.get('comment_text', '').strip()
             if not comment_text:
                 errors = ['Comment text is required.']
                 comments_list = get_comments_by_article_and_version(article_id, version_id)
                 return render_template('comments.html', article_id=article_id, version_id=version_id, comments=comments_list, errors=errors)
         
             create_comment(article_id, version_id, username, comment_text)
         
             success_msg = 'Comment added successfully.'
             comments_list = get_comments_by_article_and_version(article_id, version_id)
             return render_template('comments.html', article_id=article_id, version_id=version_id, comments=comments_list, success=success_msg)

         from flask import Flask, request, redirect, url_for, render_template, session, abort
         from datetime import datetime
         import os
         import threading
         import difflib
         
         app = Flask(__name__)
         app.secret_key = 'super_secret_key_change_me'  # Session secret key
         
         DATA_DIR = 'data'
         file_lock = threading.Lock()
         
         # Utility functions for file IO and parsing
         
         def read_pipe_delimited_file(filename, fields):
             file_path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, filename)
             data = []
             if not os.path.exists(file_path):
                 return data
             with open(file_path, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for line in f:
                     line=line.strip()
                     if not line:
                         continue
                     parts = line.split('|')
                     if len(parts) < len(fields):
                         continue
                     record = dict(zip(fields, parts))
                     data.append(record)
             return data
         
         def append_pipe_delimited_file(filename, fields, record):
             with file_lock:
                 file_path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, filename)
                 with open(file_path, 'a', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     line = '|'.join(str(record.get(fld, '')).replace('\n',' ') for fld in fields) + '\n'
                     f.write(line)
         
         def overwrite_pipe_delimited_file(filename, fields, records):
             with file_lock:
                 file_path = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, filename)
                 with open(file_path, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for rec in records:
                         line = '|'.join(str(rec.get(fld, '')).replace('\n',' ') for fld in fields) + '\n'
                         f.write(line)
         
         # Models and data file schemas
         
         # Users
         USER_FIELDS = ['id', 'username', 'role']
         def get_all_users():
             return read_pipe_delimited_file('users.txt', USER_FIELDS)
         
         def get_user_by_username(username):
             users = get_all_users()
             for user in users:
                 if user['username'] == username:
                     return user
             return None
         
         # Articles
         ARTICLE_FIELDS = ['article_id', 'title', 'author', 'category', 'status', 'created_date', 'last_modified']
         
         def get_all_articles():
             return read_pipe_delimited_file('articles.txt', ARTICLE_FIELDS)
         
         def get_article_by_id(article_id):
             articles = get_all_articles()
             for article in articles:
                 if article['article_id'] == str(article_id):
                     return article
             return None
         
         def update_article(article_id, title=None, category=None, status=None, last_modified=None):
             articles = get_all_articles()
             updated = False
             for art in articles:
                 if art['article_id'] == str(article_id):
                     if title is not None:
                         art['title'] = title
                     if category is not None:
                         art['category'] = category
                     if status is not None:
                         art['status'] = status
                     if last_modified is not None:
                         art['last_modified'] = last_modified
                     updated = True
                     break
             if updated:
                 overwrite_pipe_delimited_file('articles.txt', ARTICLE_FIELDS, articles)
             return updated
         
         def create_article(title, author, category):
             articles = get_all_articles()
             max_id = max([int(a['article_id']) for a in articles], default=0)
             new_id = str(max_id + 1)
             now_str = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')
             new_article = {
                 'article_id': new_id,
                 'title': title,
                 'author': author,
                 'category': category if category else '',
                 'status': 'draft',
                 'created_date': now_str,
                 'last_modified': now_str
             }
             append_pipe_delimited_file('articles.txt', ARTICLE_FIELDS, new_article)
             return new_id
         
         # Article Versions
         ARTICLE_VERSION_FIELDS = ['version_id','article_id','version_number','content','author','created_date','change_summary']
         
         def get_all_article_versions():
             return read_pipe_delimited_file('article_versions.txt', ARTICLE_VERSION_FIELDS)
         
         def get_versions_by_article_id(article_id):
             versions = get_all_article_versions()
             filtered = [v for v in versions if v['article_id'] == str(article_id)]
             filtered.sort(key=lambda v: int(v['version_number']))
             return filtered
         
         def get_latest_version(article_id):
             versions = get_versions_by_article_id(article_id)
             if not versions:
                 return None
             return versions[-1]
         
         def create_new_version(article_id, content, author, change_summary):
             versions = get_versions_by_article_id(article_id)
             max_version_num = max([int(v['version_number']) for v in versions], default=0)
             new_version_num = max_version_num + 1
             all_versions = get_all_article_versions()
             max_version_id = max([int(v['version_id']) for v in all_versions], default=0)
             new_version_id = max_version_id + 1
             now_str = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')
             version_record = {
                 'version_id': str(new_version_id),
                 'article_id': str(article_id),
                 'version_number': str(new_version_num),
                 'content': content,
                 'author': author,
                 'created_date': now_str,
                 'change_summary': change_summary if change_summary else ''
             }
             append_pipe_delimited_file('article_versions.txt', ARTICLE_VERSION_FIELDS, version_record)
             return version_record
         
         # Approvals
         APPROVAL_FIELDS = ['approval_id', 'article_id', 'version_id', 'approver', 'status', 'comment', 'timestamp']
         
         def get_all_approvals():
             return read_pipe_delimited_file('approvals.txt', APPROVAL_FIELDS)
         
         def get_approvals_by_article_and_version(article_id, version_id):
             approvals = get_all_approvals()
             filtered = [a for a in approvals if a['article_id'] == str(article_id) and a['version_id'] == str(version_id)]
             return filtered
         
         def create_approval(article_id, version_id, approver, status, comment):
             approvals = get_all_approvals()
             max_id = max([int(a['approval_id']) for a in approvals], default=0)
             new_id = str(max_id + 1)
             now_str = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')
             approval_record = {
                 'approval_id': new_id,
                 'article_id': str(article_id),
                 'version_id': str(version_id),
                 'approver': approver,
                 'status': status,
                 'comment': comment if comment else '',
                 'timestamp': now_str
             }
             append_pipe_delimited_file('approvals.txt', APPROVAL_FIELDS, approval_record)
             return approval_record
         
         # Comments
         COMMENT_FIELDS = ['comment_id', 'article_id', 'version_id', 'author', 'comment_text', 'timestamp']
         
         def get_all_comments():
             return read_pipe_delimited_file('comments.txt', COMMENT_FIELDS)
         
         def get_comments_by_article_and_version(article_id, version_id):
             comments = get_all_comments()
             filtered = [c for c in comments if c['article_id'] == str(article_id) and c['version_id'] == str(version_id)]
             filtered.sort(key=lambda c: c['timestamp'])
             return filtered
         
         def create_comment(article_id, version_id, author, comment_text):
             comments = get_all_comments()
             max_id = max([int(c['comment_id']) for c in comments], default=0)
             new_id = str(max_id + 1)
             now_str = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')
             comment_record = {
                 'comment_id': new_id,
                 'article_id': str(article_id),
                 'version_id': str(version_id),
                 'author': author,
                 'comment_text': comment_text if comment_text else '',
                 'timestamp': now_str
             }
             append_pipe_delimited_file('comments.txt', COMMENT_FIELDS, comment_record)
             return comment_record
         
         # Workflow stages
         WORKFLOW_FIELDS = ['stage_id', 'name', 'category', 'required_reviewers']
         
         def get_all_workflow_stages():
             return read_pipe_delimited_file('workflow_stages.txt', WORKFLOW_FIELDS)
         
         # Analytics
         ANALYTICS_FIELDS = ['analytics_id', 'article_id', 'views', 'unique_visitors', 'avg_time_on_article', 'shares', 'date']
         
         def get_all_analytics():
             return read_pipe_delimited_file('analytics.txt', ANALYTICS_FIELDS)
         
         def get_analytics_by_article(article_id):
             analytics = get_all_analytics()
             filtered = [a for a in analytics if a['article_id'] == str(article_id)]
             return filtered
         
         def aggregate_analytics(article_id):
             records = get_analytics_by_article(article_id)
             total_views = 0
             unique_dates = set()
             total_time = 0
             total_shares = 0
             count = 0
             for rec in records:
                 try:
                     total_views += int(rec['views'])
                 except:
                     pass
                 unique_dates.add(rec['date'])
                 try:
                     total_time += float(rec['avg_time_on_article'])
                 except:
                     pass
                 try:
                     total_shares += int(rec['shares'])
                 except:
                     pass
                 count += 1
             avg_time = (total_time/count) if count > 0 else 0
             analytics_summary = {
                 'total_views': total_views,
                 'unique_visitors_count': len(unique_dates),
                 'average_time_on_article': round(avg_time, 2),
                 'total_shares': total_shares
             }
             return analytics_summary
         
         # Version diff generation
         
         def generate_diff_summary(old_content, new_content):
             old_lines = old_content.splitlines()
             new_lines = new_content.splitlines()
             diff = difflib.unified_diff(old_lines, new_lines, fromfile='old', tofile='new', lineterm='')
             return '\n'.join(diff)
         
         # Simulate user session retrieval
         
         def get_logged_in_username():
             if 'username' in session:
                 return session['username']
             return None
         
         
         # Routes
         @app.route('/')
         def index():
             return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))
         
         @app.route('/dashboard', methods=['GET'])
         def dashboard():
             username = get_logged_in_username()
             if not username:
                 return redirect(url_for('index'))
         
             all_articles = get_all_articles()
             user_articles = [a for a in all_articles if a['author'] == username]
             published_count = len([a for a in user_articles if a['status'] == 'published'])
             approval_count = len([a for a in user_articles if a['status'] == 'in_approval'])
         
             quick_stats = {
                 'total_articles': len(user_articles),
                 'published_articles': published_count,
                 'in_approval_articles': approval_count
             }
         
             recent_activity_raw = sorted(user_articles, key=lambda x: x['last_modified'], reverse=True)[:5]
             recent_activity = []
             for art in recent_activity_raw:
                 recent_activity.append({
                     'article_id': art['article_id'],
                     'title': art['title'],
                     'status': art['status'],
                     'last_modified': art['last_modified']
                 })
         
             return render_template('dashboard.html', username=username, quick_stats=quick_stats, recent_activity=recent_activity)
         
         @app.route('/article/create', methods=['GET','POST'])
         def create_article_route():
             username = get_logged_in_username()
             if not username:
                 return redirect(url_for('index'))
             if request.method == 'GET':
                 return render_template('article_create.html')
         
             # POST
             title = request.form.get('article_title','').strip()
             content = request.form.get('article_content','').strip()
             category = request.form.get('category','').strip()
             errors = []
             if not title:
                 errors.append('Title is required.')
             if not content:
                 errors.append('Content is required.')
             if errors:
                 return render_template('article_create.html', errors=errors, article_title=title, article_content=content, category=category)
         
             new_article_id = create_article(title, username, category)
             create_new_version(new_article_id, content, username, change_summary='Initial version')
             success_message = 'Article created successfully.'
             return render_template('article_create.html', success=success_message)
         
         @app.route('/article/<int:article_id>/edit', methods=['GET','POST'])
         def edit_article(article_id):
             username = get_logged_in_username()
             if not username:
                 return redirect(url_for('index'))
         
             article = get_article_by_id(article_id)
             if not article:
                 abort(404, description='Article not found')
             if article['author'] != username:
                 abort(403, description='Permission denied: can only edit your own articles.')
         
             if request.method == 'GET':
                 latest_version = get_latest_version(article_id)
                 title = article['title']
                 content = latest_version['content'] if latest_version else ''
                 return render_template('article_edit.html', article_id=article_id, title=title, content=content)
         
             # POST
             new_title = request.form.get('article_title','').strip()
             content = request.form.get('article_content','').strip()
             category = request.form.get('category','').strip()
             change_summary = request.form.get('change_summary','').strip()
         
             errors = []
             if not new_title:
                 errors.append('Title is required.')
             if not content:
                 errors.append('Content is required.')
             if not change_summary:
                 errors.append('Change summary is required.')
             if errors:
                 return render_template('article_edit.html', article_id=article_id, title=new_title, content=content, errors=errors)
         
             create_new_version(article_id, content, username, change_summary)
             now_str = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')
             update_article(article_id, title=new_title, category=category if category else None, last_modified=now_str)
             success_message = 'Article updated and new version saved successfully.'
             return render_template('article_edit.html', article_id=article_id, title=new_title, content=content, success=success_message)
         
         @app.route('/article/<int:article_id>/versions', methods=['GET'])
         def article_version_history(article_id):
             username = get_logged_in_username()
             if not username:
                 return redirect(url_for('index'))
             article = get_article_by_id(article_id)
             if not article:
                 abort(404, description='Article not found')
         
             versions = get_versions_by_article_id(article_id)
             versions_sorted = sorted(versions, key=lambda v: int(v['version_number']))
             current_version = max([int(v['version_number']) for v in versions], default=0)
         
             comparison = {}
             for i in range(1, len(versions_sorted)):
                 old_v = versions_sorted[i-1]
                 new_v = versions_sorted[i]
                 diff_summary = generate_diff_summary(old_v['content'], new_v['content'])
                 key = f"{old_v['version_number']}_to_{new_v['version_number']}"
                 comparison[key] = diff_summary
         
             return render_template('article_versions.html', article_id=article_id, versions=versions_sorted, comparison=comparison, current_version=current_version)
         
         @app.route('/articles/mine', methods=['GET'])
         def my_articles():
             username = get_logged_in_username()
             if not username:
                 return redirect(url_for('index'))
             filter_status = request.args.get('status','').strip().lower()
             articles = get_all_articles()
             user_articles = [a for a in articles if a['author'] == username]
             if filter_status:
                 user_articles = [a for a in user_articles if a['status'].lower() == filter_status]
             return render_template('articles_mine.html', articles=user_articles, filter_status=filter_status)
         
         @app.route('/articles/published', methods=['GET'])
         def published_articles():
             filter_category = request.args.get('filter_category','').strip().lower()
             sort_option = request.args.get('sort_option','').strip().lower()
             articles = get_all_articles()
             published = [a for a in articles if a['status'] == 'published']
             if filter_category:
                 published = [a for a in published if a['category'].lower() == filter_category]
             if sort_option == 'date_desc':
                 published.sort(key=lambda a: a['created_date'], reverse=True)
             elif sort_option == 'date_asc':
                 published.sort(key=lambda a: a['created_date'])
             elif sort_option == 'title_asc':
                 published.sort(key=lambda a: a['title'].lower())
             elif sort_option == 'title_desc':
                 published.sort(key=lambda a: a['title'].lower(), reverse=True)
             return render_template('articles_published.html', articles=published, filter_category=filter_category, sort_option=sort_option)
         
         @app.route('/calendar', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def content_calendar():
             username = get_logged_in_username()
             if not username:
                 return redirect(url_for('index'))
         
             calendar_view = 'month'  # Default view
             calendar_data = []  # Placeholder for calendar events or schedules
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 event_name = request.form.get('event_name', '').strip()
                 event_date = request.form.get('event_date', '').strip()
                 # No storage specified for calendar events in design, so this is a stub
                 success_message = f'Event "{event_name}" added successfully (stub, not persisted).'
                 return render_template('calendar.html', calendar_view=calendar_view, calendar_data=calendar_data, success=success_message)
         
             return render_template('calendar.html', calendar_view=calendar_view, calendar_data=calendar_data)
         
         @app.route('/article/<int:article_id>/analytics', methods=['GET'])
         def article_analytics(article_id):
             username = get_logged_in_username()
             if not username:
                 return redirect(url_for('index'))
             article = get_article_by_id(article_id)
             if not article:
                 abort(404, description='Article not found')
         
             analytics_summary = aggregate_analytics(article_id)
             return render_template('article_analytics.html', article_id=article_id, analytics=analytics_summary)
         
         # Approval POST endpoint
         @app.route('/article/<int:article_id>/version/<int:version_id>/approve', methods=['POST'])
         def approve_version(article_id, version_id):
             username = get_logged_in_username()
             if not username:
                 return redirect(url_for('index'))
             status = request.form.get('status', '').strip().lower()
             comment = request.form.get('comment', '').strip()
             if status not in ['approved', 'rejected', 'revision_requested']:
                 return {'error': 'Invalid approval status'}, 400
             approval_record = create_approval(article_id, version_id, username, status, comment)
             # Business logic to advance workflow could be added here
             return {'message': 'Approval recorded', 'approval': approval_record}, 200
         
         # Comments endpoint GET and POST
         @app.route('/article/<int:article_id>/version/<int:version_id>/comments', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def article_version_comments(article_id, version_id):
             username = get_logged_in_username()
             if not username:
                 return redirect(url_for('index'))
         
             if request.method == 'GET':
                 comments_list = get_comments_by_article_and_version(article_id, version_id)
                 return render_template('comments.html', article_id=article_id, version_id=version_id, comments=comments_list)
         
             # POST add comment
             comment_text = request.form.get('comment_text', '').strip()
             if not comment_text:
                 errors = ['Comment text is required.']
                 comments_list = get_comments_by_article_and_version(article_id, version_id)
                 return render_template('comments.html', article_id=article_id, version_id=version_id, comments=comments_list, errors=errors)
         
             create_comment(article_id, version_id, username, comment_text)
             success_message = 'Comment added successfully.'
             comments_list = get_comments_by_article_and_version(article_id, version_id)
             return render_template('comments.html', article_id=article_id, version_id=version_id, comments=comments_list, success=success_message)
         
         # End of app.py

         from flask import Flask, request, redirect, url_for, render_template, session, abort
         from datetime import datetime
         import os
         import threading
         import difflib
         
         # Flask app initialization
         app = Flask(__name__)
         app.secret_key = 'a_very_secret_key_for_session_management_change_me'  # For session management
         
         DATA_DIR = 'data'
         LOCK = threading.Lock()  # Global lock for file write operations
         
         # Helper function to parse pipe-delimited text files into list of dicts
         # fields is a list of field names
         
         def read_pipe_delimited_file(filename, fields):
             records = []
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, filename)
             if not os.path.exists(filepath):
                 return records
             with open(filepath, 'r', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                 for line in f:
                     line=line.strip()
                     if not line:
                         continue
                     parts = line.split('|')
                     if len(parts) < len(fields):
                         # malformed line - skip
                         continue
                     rec = dict(zip(fields, parts))
                     records.append(rec)
             return records
         
         # Helper function to append a record (dict) to pipe-delimited file
         # fields order needed
         
         def append_pipe_delimited_file(filename, fields, record):
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, filename)
             with LOCK:
                 with open(filepath, 'a', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     line = '|'.join(str(record.get(field, '')).replace('\n',' ') for field in fields) + '\n'
                     f.write(line)
         
         # Helper function to overwrite whole file (list of dicts)
         def overwrite_pipe_delimited_file(filename, fields, records):
             filepath = os.path.join(DATA_DIR, filename)
             with LOCK:
                 with open(filepath, 'w', encoding='utf-8') as f:
                     for record in records:
                         line = '|'.join(str(record.get(field, '')).replace('\n',' ') for field in fields) + '\n'
                         f.write(line)
         
         ############################
         # User Model
         ############################
         # users.txt fields:
         # id|username|role
         USER_FIELDS = ['id','username','role']
         
         def get_all_users():
             return read_pipe_delimited_file('users.txt', USER_FIELDS)
         
         def get_user_by_username(username):
             users = get_all_users()
             for u in users:
                 if u['username'] == username:
                     return u
             return None
         
         ############################
         # Article Model
         ############################
         # articles.txt fields:
         # article_id|title|author|category|status|created_date|last_modified
         ARTICLE_FIELDS = ['article_id','title','author','category','status','created_date','last_modified']
         
         def get_all_articles():
             return read_pipe_delimited_file('articles.txt', ARTICLE_FIELDS)
         
         def get_article_by_id(article_id):
             articles = get_all_articles()
             for a in articles:
                 if a['article_id'] == str(article_id):
                     return a
             return None
         
         # Update article in articles.txt by article_id
         def update_article(article_id, title=None, category=None, status=None, last_modified=None):
             articles = get_all_articles()
             updated = False
             for a in articles:
                 if a['article_id'] == str(article_id):
                     if title is not None:
                         a['title'] = title
                     if category is not None:
                         a['category'] = category
                     if status is not None:
                         a['status'] = status
                     if last_modified is not None:
                         a['last_modified'] = last_modified
                     updated = True
                     break
             if updated:
                 overwrite_pipe_delimited_file('articles.txt', ARTICLE_FIELDS, articles)
             return updated
         
         # Create new article
         # Returns article_id assigned
         # article_id assigned auto-increment max existing + 1
         
         def create_article(title, author, category):
             articles = get_all_articles()
             if articles:
                 max_id = max(int(a['article_id']) for a in articles)
             else:
                 max_id = 0
             new_id = max_id + 1
             now_str = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')
             new_article = {
                 'article_id': str(new_id),
                 'title': title,
                 'author': author,
                 'category': category if category else '',
                 'status': 'draft',
                 'created_date': now_str,
                 'last_modified': now_str
             }
             append_pipe_delimited_file('articles.txt', ARTICLE_FIELDS, new_article)
             return new_id
         
         ############################
         # Article Versions Model
         ############################
         # article_versions.txt fields:
         # version_id|article_id|version_number|content|author|created_date|change_summary
         ARTICLE_VERSION_FIELDS = ['version_id','article_id','version_number','content','author','created_date','change_summary']
         
         def get_all_article_versions():
             return read_pipe_delimited_file('article_versions.txt', ARTICLE_VERSION_FIELDS)
         
         def get_versions_by_article_id(article_id):
             versions = get_all_article_versions()
             result = [v for v in versions if v['article_id'] == str(article_id)]
             # Sort by version_number ascending
             result.sort(key=lambda x: int(x['version_number']))
             return result
         
         # Get latest version for article_id
         # returns None if none found
         
         def get_latest_version(article_id):
             versions = get_versions_by_article_id(article_id)
             if not versions:
                 return None
             return versions[-1]
         
         # Create new version for article
         # version_number auto-incremented
         
         def create_new_version(article_id, content, author, change_summary):
             versions = get_versions_by_article_id(article_id)
             if versions:
                 max_version = max(int(v['version_number']) for v in versions)
             else:
                 max_version = 0
             new_version_num = max_version + 1
             # version_id assigned as max existing + 1 (global)
             all_versions = get_all_article_versions()
             if all_versions:
                 max_version_id = max(int(v['version_id']) for v in all_versions)
             else:
                 max_version_id = 0
             new_version_id = max_version_id + 1
             now_str = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')
             new_version = {
                 'version_id': str(new_version_id),
                 'article_id': str(article_id),
                 'version_number': str(new_version_num),
                 'content': content,
                 'author': author,
                 'created_date': now_str,
                 'change_summary': change_summary if change_summary else ''
             }
             append_pipe_delimited_file('article_versions.txt', ARTICLE_VERSION_FIELDS, new_version)
             return new_version

         # Append new comment

         ############################

         WORKFLOW_FIELDS = ['stage_id','name','category','required_reviewers']
         
         def get_all_workflow_stages():
             return read_pipe_delimited_file('workflow_stages.txt', WORKFLOW_FIELDS)
         
         ############################
         # Analytics Model
         ############################
         # analytics.txt fields:
         # analytics_id|article_id|views|unique_visitors|avg_time_on_article|shares|date
         ANALYTICS_FIELDS = ['analytics_id','article_id','views','unique_visitors','avg_time_on_article','shares','date']
         
         def get_all_analytics():
             return read_pipe_delimited_file('analytics.txt', ANALYTICS_FIELDS)
         
         def get_analytics_by_article(article_id):
             analytics = get_all_analytics()
             filtered = [a for a in analytics if a['article_id'] == str(article_id)]
             return filtered
         
         # Aggregate analytics for an article across all dates
         
         def aggregate_analytics(article_id):
             records = get_analytics_by_article(article_id)
             total_views = 0
             unique_visitors_set = set()
             total_time = 0.0
             total_shares = 0
             count = 0
             for rec in records:
                 total_views += int(rec['views']) if rec['views'].isdigit() else 0
                 unique_visitors_set.add(rec['date'])  # Count unique days as proxy for unique visitors
                 try:
                     t = float(rec['avg_time_on_article'])
                 except:
                     t = 0
                 total_time += t
                 total_shares += int(rec['shares']) if rec['shares'].isdigit() else 0
                 count += 1
             avg_time = (total_time/count) if count > 0 else 0
             analytics_summary = {
                 'total_views': total_views,
                 'unique_visitors_count': len(unique_visitors_set),
                 'average_time_on_article': round(avg_time,2),
                 'total_shares': total_shares
             }
             return analytics_summary
         
         ############################
         # Version Control Util Functions
         ############################
         # Generate diff summary between two versions (old_content, new_content)
         def generate_diff_summary(old_content, new_content):
             old_lines = old_content.splitlines()
             new_lines = new_content.splitlines()
             diff = difflib.unified_diff(old_lines, new_lines, lineterm='')
             diff_text = '\n'.join(diff)
             # For brevity, just return diff as a string
             return diff_text
         
         ############################
         # Authentication & Session Helpers
         ############################
         # For demonstration, simulate logged in user from session
         
         def get_logged_in_username():
             # In real app, use flask-login or similar
             if 'username' in session:
                 return session['username']
             return None
         
         ############################
         # Routes Implementation
         ############################
         
         @app.route('/')
         def root_redirect():
             return redirect(url_for('dashboard'))
         
         
         @app.route('/dashboard')
         def dashboard():
             username = get_logged_in_username()
             if not username:
                 return redirect(url_for('root_redirect'))
             # Quick stats and recent activity for user
             # Quick stats: number of articles user authored, articles published, articles in approval
             all_articles = get_all_articles()
             user_articles = [a for a in all_articles if a['author'] == username]
             published_count = sum(1 for a in user_articles if a['status'] == 'published')
             in_approval_count = sum(1 for a in user_articles if a['status'] == 'in_approval')
             quick_stats = {
                 'total_articles': len(user_articles),
                 'published_articles': published_count,
                 'in_approval_articles': in_approval_count
             }
             # Recent activity: last 5 edited or created articles
             user_articles_sorted = sorted(user_articles, key=lambda a: a['last_modified'], reverse=True)[:5]
             recent_activity = []
             for a in user_articles_sorted:
                 recent_activity.append({
                     'article_id': a['article_id'],
                     'title': a['title'],
                     'status': a['status'],
                     'last_modified': a['last_modified']
                 })
             # Render dashboard template with these variables
             return render_template('dashboard.html', username=username, quick_stats=quick_stats, recent_activity=recent_activity)
         
         
         @app.route('/article/create', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def create_article():
             username = get_logged_in_username()
             if not username:
                 return redirect(url_for('root_redirect'))
         
             if request.method == 'GET':
                 return render_template('article_create.html')
         
             # POST method
             title = request.form.get('article_title', '').strip()
             content = request.form.get('article_content', '').strip()
             category = request.form.get('category', '').strip()  # Optional category
         
             errors = []
             if not title:
                 errors.append('Title is required.')
             if not content:
                 errors.append('Content is required.')
         
             if errors:
                 return render_template('article_create.html', errors=errors, article_title=title, article_content=content, category=category)
         
             # Create article record
             new_article_id = create_article(title, username, category)
         
             # Create initial version with version 1
             change_summary = 'Initial version'
             create_new_version(new_article_id, content, username, change_summary)
         
             success_msg = 'Article created successfully.'
             return render_template('article_create.html', success=success_msg)
         
         
         @app.route('/article/<int:article_id>/edit', methods=['GET','POST'])
         def edit_article(article_id):
             username = get_logged_in_username()
             if not username:
                 return redirect(url_for('root_redirect'))
         
             article = get_article_by_id(article_id)
             if not article:
                 abort(404, description='Article not found')
             if article['author'] != username:
                 abort(403, description='Permission denied. Can only edit your own articles.')
         
             if request.method == 'GET':
                 # Load latest version content
                 latest_version = get_latest_version(article_id)
                 content = latest_version['content'] if latest_version else ''
                 title = article['title']
                 return render_template('article_edit.html', article_id=article_id, title=title, content=content)
         
             # POST method
             new_title = request.form.get('article_title', '').strip()
             content = request.form.get('article_content', '').strip()
             category = request.form.get('category', '').strip()  # optional
             change_summary = request.form.get('change_summary', '').strip()  # descriptive summary of edits
         
             errors = []
             if not new_title:
                 errors.append('Title is required.')
             if not content:
                 errors.append('Content is required.')
             if not change_summary:
                 errors.append('Change summary is required.')
         
             if errors:
                 return render_template('article_edit.html', article_id=article_id, title=new_title, content=content, errors=errors)
         
             # Save new version
             new_version = create_new_version(article_id, content, username, change_summary)
         
             # Update article title, category and last_modified date
             now_str = datetime.now().strftime('%Y-%m-%d %H:%M:%S')
             update_article(article_id, title=new_title, category=category if category else None, last_modified=now_str)
         
             success_msg = 'Article updated and new version saved successfully.'
             return render_template('article_edit.html', article_id=article_id, title=new_title, content=content, success=success_msg)
         
         
         @app.route('/article/<int:article_id>/versions', methods=['GET'])
         def article_version_history(article_id):
             username = get_logged_in_username()
             if not username:
                 return redirect(url_for('root_redirect'))
         
             article = get_article_by_id(article_id)
             if not article:
                 abort(404, description='Article not found')
         
             versions = get_versions_by_article_id(article_id)
             if not versions:
                 versions = []
             # current_version is the highest version number
             current_version = max((int(v['version_number']) for v in versions), default=0)
         
             # Prepare a comparison dict with diffs for each pair of consecutive versions
             comparison = {}
             for i in range(1, len(versions)):
                 v_old = versions[i-1]
                 v_new = versions[i]
                 diff_summary = generate_diff_summary(v_old['content'], v_new['content'])
                 comparison_key = f"{v_old['version_number']}_to_{v_new['version_number']}"
                 comparison[comparison_key] = diff_summary
         
             return render_template('article_versions.html',
                                    article_id=article_id,
                                    versions=versions,
                                    comparison=comparison,
                                    current_version=current_version)
         
         
         @app.route('/articles/mine', methods=['GET'])
         def my_articles():
             username = get_logged_in_username()
             if not username:
                 return redirect(url_for('root_redirect'))
         
             filter_status = request.args.get('status', '').strip().lower()
             all_articles = get_all_articles()
             user_articles = [a for a in all_articles if a['author'] == username]
         
             if filter_status:
                 user_articles = [a for a in user_articles if a['status'].lower() == filter_status]
         
             # Render with articles and filter_status
             return render_template('articles_mine.html', articles=user_articles, filter_status=filter_status)
         
         
         @app.route('/articles/published', methods=['GET'])
         def published_articles():
             filter_category = request.args.get('filter_category', '').strip().lower()
             sort_option = request.args.get('sort_option', '').strip().lower()
         
             all_articles = get_all_articles()
             published_articles = [a for a in all_articles if a['status'] == 'published']
         
             if filter_category:
                 published_articles = [a for a in published_articles if a['category'].lower() == filter_category]
         
             if sort_option == 'date_desc':
                 published_articles.sort(key=lambda a: a['created_date'], reverse=True)
             elif sort_option == 'date_asc':
                 published_articles.sort(key=lambda a: a['created_date'])
             elif sort_option == 'title_asc':
                 published_articles.sort(key=lambda a: a['title'].lower())
             elif sort_option == 'title_desc':
                 published_articles.sort(key=lambda a: a['title'].lower(), reverse=True)
         
             return render_template('articles_published.html',
                                    articles=published_articles,
                                    filter_category=filter_category,
                                    sort_option=sort_option)
         
         
         @app.route('/calendar', methods=['GET','POST'])
         def content_calendar():
             username = get_logged_in_username()
             if not username:
                 return redirect(url_for('root_redirect'))
         
             # For this app, we don't have detail of calendar event schema
             # We keep a simple calendar_data list stored in memory or loaded/saved from a file events.txt (not specified)
             # Here we simulate with empty or fixed data
         
             calendar_data = []
             calendar_view = 'month'  # For example
         
             if request.method == 'POST':
                 # For demonstration, read new event data from form (e.g., event_name, date)
                 event_name = request.form.get('event_name', '').strip()
                 event_date = request.form.get('event_date', '').strip()
                 # Normally, would add event to persistent storage, but data file schema not defined, so this is stub
                 # Return calendar with confirmation
                 success_msg = 'Event added successfully (stub, not persisted)'
                 return render_template('calendar.html', calendar_view=calendar_view, calendar_data=calendar_data, success=success_msg)
         
             return render_template('calendar.html', calendar_view=calendar_view, calendar_data=calendar_data)
         
         
         @app.route('/article/<int:article_id>/analytics', methods=['GET'])
         def article_analytics(article_id):
             username = get_logged_in_username()
             if not username:
                 return redirect(url_for('root_redirect'))

         # Additional routes for approval and comments for completeness
         
         @app.route('/article/<int:article_id>/version/<int:version_id>/approve', methods=['POST'])
         def approve_version(article_id, version_id):
             username = get_logged_in_username()
             if not username:
                 return redirect(url_for('root_redirect'))
         
             status = request.form.get('status','').strip().lower()  # expected: approved, rejected, revision_requested
             comment = request.form.get('comment','').strip()
             if status not in ['approved','rejected','revision_requested']:
                 return {'error': 'Invalid status value'}, 400
         
             approval = create_approval(article_id, version_id, username, status, comment)
         
             # Service logic to move article through workflow stages would go here (not implemented in full)
         
             return {'message': 'Approval recorded', 'approval': approval}, 200
         
         
         @app.route('/article/<int:article_id>/version/<int:version_id>/comments', methods=['GET', 'POST'])
         def comments(article_id, version_id):
             username = get_logged_in_username()
             if not username:
                 return redirect(url_for('root_redirect'))
         
             if request.method == 'GET':
                 comments_list = get_comments_by_article_and_version(article_id, version_id)
                 return render_template('comments.html', article_id=article_id, version_id=version_id, comments=comments_list)
         
             # POST method to add comment
             comment_text = request.form.get('comment_text', '').strip()
             if not comment_text:
                 errors = ['Comment text is required.']
                 comments_list = get_comments_by_article_and_version(article_id, version_id)
                 return render_template('comments.html', article_id=article_id, version_id=version_id, comments=comments_list, errors=errors)
         
             create_comment(article_id, version_id, username, comment_text)
         
             success_msg = 'Comment added successfully.'
             comments_list = get_comments_by_article_and_version(article_id, version_id)
             return render_template('comments.html', article_id=article_id, version_id=version_id, comments=comments_list, success=success_msg)
